        <div id="content-wrapper">
            <span class="content">
                <a role="button" id="close-help" data-tip-page="8">x</a>
                <p>Your recipe index is automatically created as you add books, magazines and blogs to your Bookshelf. The Library is an index of all the recipes.      </p>
<p>Many recipes have <a href="http://support.eatyourbooks.com/customer/portal/articles/1031706-searching-online-recipes-in-the-eyb-library" target="_blank">online links</a> - you can add any of these to your Bookshelf.     </p>
<p>See large images in <strong>Gallery View</strong> - use <strong>View As</strong> button below to alter your view.     </p>
<p>You can add any recipe you find on any other food website by using the <a href="http://support.eatyourbooks.com/customer/portal/articles/1031712-adding-a-recipe-from-a-food-website-to-my-bookshelf-using-the-bookmarklet" target="_blank">Bookmarklet</a> feature.    </p>
<p>Narrow your search by selecting ingredients, cuisine, and more in the <a href="http://support.eatyourbooks.com/customer/portal/articles/1031669-searching-for-recipes-that-use-specific-ingredients" target="_blank">Filter By</a> box.  </p>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var entityRoot = 'Recipe';        
    $(function () {
        var rs = $("#results-list");
        attachBookshelfHandler(rs);
        attachRatingHandler(rs);
        attachRequestIndexHandler(rs);
        attachBuyBookHandler(rs);
        attachLinkedBooksHandler(rs);
        attachAddBookmarkHandler(rs, entityRoot, ".listing");
        setupMainSearch(false);
        setupVideoPopup();

        var $container = $("#gallery-view");
        $container.imagesLoaded(function () {
            $container.masonry({
                itemSelector: ".gallery-item",
                columnWidth: 210,
                gutterWidth: 20
            });
            $container.css("visibility", "visible");
        });
    });
</script>
